I recently received reports from the guides about the fruit platter that‚Äôs stale/not edible to eat. I did my observation in the past 3 days and all the guides already follow the instructions to always put in the ice box and why is it still stale? The answer is the temperature and hygiene, the best temperature to put it in is about 3-7 degree Celsius, to be honest it‚Äôs hard to maintain the temperature since it‚Äôs only ice box and I found out that our chiller at the office was not that in a good temperature and‚Ä¶ as far as I know the supplier prep and delivery the fruits in the evening, the perfect time to deliver is in early morning(fresh cut). Those might be the reasons why the fruits are easily to get stale especially if we mixed the fruits in one plate together. In my opinion it‚Äôs better to try just to have 1 color per plate for example red watermelon and yellow watermelon will look tempting for the guests rather than mixed fruits in one plate.

[05/11/24, 10.04.38] Ibu Rhiry From Nemo Food Supply: The difference between laser and UV printing:

UV printing can be in color, and the result from our machine is raised, unlike screen printing, which is flat with the bottle surface. It‚Äôs more expensive because it uses ink, starting at 80,000 IDR per position, depending on the position and size of the logo, as well as the print duration.

Laser printing, on the other hand, produces a silver result, showing the base color of the stainless bottle. The color coating is burned off to reveal the silver underneath. This starts at 60,000 IDR per position, also depending on the duration, logo size, and position.
